 History of Dhule Lok Sabha seat
 
 
 yadi dhule loksabhaa seat ke itihaas par najar daali jaae to 1957 main yahaan sabase pehla chunaav hua tha
 It was here that Patil, who won the Uttamrao signs of the Bharatiya Jana Sangh, came
 lekin 1962 ke chunaav main yahaan congress ne aisi baaji palati ki koi doosraa dal 35 saal tak satta hasil nahin kar paaya

 iske baad 1977 main vijay naval patil yahaan satta main aae
 After him, in 1980, Reshma Motiram Bhoye came from here winning Congress ticket for the first time
 unhone 1984 or 1989 main do chunaav lagaataar jitkar hetric banaai
 After him, Bapu Hari Chaure won here in the 1991 Lok Sabha elections

 '' bharat tibet seemaa police (itibipi) main kisi bhi tarah kii bhartee ke liye abhyarthiyon ko bhartee kendron ke ab chakkar nahin kaatane padenge
 For this, ITBP has launched integrated web portals
 sashastr sainya balon main apane tarah ke pehle webportal kii madad se group di main driver or bawarchi se lekar inspector or doctor evam ejeeniyar sahit tamaam padon par bhartee ke liye aavedan kiya ja sakegaa
 ITBP Inspector General Krishna Chaudhary recently started this web portal and also linked this initiative to paperless armed forces
 isaki khaasiyat yah he ki icchhuk abhyarthi ko portal par apana mahaj ek profile bananaa hoga
 According to the educational qualification recorded in the profile, he will be automatically told from the portal which positions he is eligible to recruit in ITBP
 iske baad uski yogyata ke mutabik aavedan prakriya shuru hone par abhyarthi ko email or mobile phone par alert ke jariye bhartee main shaamil hone kii soochna de di jaayegi
 ITBP spokesman Vivek Kumar Pandey said that due to this facility started for the first time in the country for recruitment in the Armed Forces, candidates will not have to repeatedly apply for various posts
 isse na sirf abhyarthiyon kii sahuuliyat badi he balki bhartee prakriya main paardarshita sunishchit hone se ise gadabadi kii shikayaton ke kaaran vilambit hone se bachaaya ja sakegaa
 Describing it as a "recruitment by ITBP candidates" service, Pandey said that the pilot project of this portal developed by the National Information Center (NIC) was started last year
 portal main darj data ke durupyog ko rokane ke liye sabhi pukhta intjaam karne ke baad ise ab shuru kiya gaya he
 Once the login ID is created on the portal, the candidate will have to go to the nearest recruitment center only for medical and physical examination during recruitment
 doordaraj ke ilaakon main icchhuk ummidavaaron ko is seva se jodne ke liye itibipi ne apane kshetreey karyaalayon (frontier jone) ko is portal se joda he

 ) itibipi ke pravaktaa vivek kumaar pandey ne bataaya ki sashastr balon main bhartee ke liye desh main pehali baar shuru hui is suvidha kii vajah se abhyarthiyon ko baar-baar vibhinn padon ke liye aavedan nahin karnaa padegaa
 This has not only increased the convenience of the candidates but also ensures transparency in the recruitment process, so that it can be avoided due to grievance complaints
 pandey ne ise ‘‘bhartee ke liye itibipi abhyarthi ke dwaara’’ seva bataate huye kaha ki rashtriya soochna kendra (enaisi) dwaara viksit is portal kaa payalat project pichley saal shuru kiya gaya tha
